<user_name>Algin Ghatcher< /user_name><Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
When sales people come to visit at work they tend to bring Lady Di's cookies - it is such a happy treat for the lab! Finally got the chance to visit the place myself... and it did not disappoint.

Location wise - not hard to find and along the old road. Small store, not much but a display and cashier. Parking was fine it's a big plaza so there's bound to be a spot for you.

Service was friendly and quick... they had tons of options and it was already 4 in the afternoon...

I needed some dessert for my GodMothers birthday - didn't think I needed that many so I got 1/2 a dozen of cupcakes and 1/2 dozen cookies. cookies here are delicious! Oreo crave is my go to but my absolute favorite has to be the oatmeal chocolate chip. Their cookies are $1.50 each but they're pretty big so the price makes sense. Their cupcakes were delicious as well and their were some fun flavors I definitely had to try... banana cream pie was good. Wasn't too sweet so I enjoyed it a lot. They had a blueberry lemon and I thought it was pretty good... I didn't think their cupcakes were overwhelming, so they were a perfect purchase for a group of older folk not looking for some something TOO sweet. They were $3 per cupcake which is pretty standard at a shop like this.

Didn't mind the price and would come back here again.< /Text>

<Rating>1< /Rating><text>Sunshine's river rafting uses false advertisement. They claim that there's lots of Rapids and that it's an enjoyable experience. What they don't tell you is ,there is one quick flow spot ,where a person sits with a camera to take your picture at that one five foot long stretch of quicker flow not even Rapids. What they don't tell you is the rest of the river is so low you have to get out and carry 150 lbs raft across multiple spots that are barely one foot deep. Will never be a returning customer. The trip has also been shortened over the years. The float used to take you all the way down to Orange Blossom now they kick you out at Horseshoe Bend or sooner depending on the flow. The shuttle service is very unsatisfactory< /text><pics>None</pics>< resp>
{'time': 1545588263571, 'text': 'Hi Kenneth,\n\nFirst, I want to say thanks for taking the time to go online and rate our services.  We are, of course, disappointed that you didn\'t enjoy the trip.  I would like to address some items in your review (just for clarification for people reading):\n\n-After a little research on our end, you appear to have gone rafting in late May/early June of 2015 (3 and a half years ago).  2015 was the very peak of the severe drought that impacted almost every river in Northern CA (including our Stanislaus River).  Because of that, there were special rules in 2015 with the lower water levels.\n\n-Since 2015, we\'ve had  stronger water years, and flows have been 2-10x as high as you saw in 2015.\n\n-We only end our trip at Horseshoe Park during very low water years, because it simply takes far too long to go to Orange Blossom.  The last three summers (2016-2018), all trips have taken out at Orange Blossom Park, and based on water levels, that should continue for at least the next couple of seasons.\n\nWe are sorry you caught us on a low water year- they aren\'t nearly as fun as when water levels are average or above!  We now post all up to date on our website RaftAdventure.com under the "Water levels/flow" section.\n\nFeel free to reach out to us at info@raftadventure.com and we can try to set your group up with a trip at a flow that you might find more ideal.'}<//resp>

< Review>
We had the most pleasant day last month, rafting down the Stanislaus river with Sunshine Rafting Adventures Knights Ferry. This was my first experience in rafting. Their equipment is first class, very stable and safe. Friendly staff, polite and experienced in the sport. We started with a safety briefing, and launched our raft, four of us on board. Took us five mn to figure out the strategy, and down the river we went. They even have a photographer at the rapids who took beautiful pictures of our crew, making lasting memories. The river is beautiful at that spot. Surrounded by green trees and grasses, although we are in a drought. Fish everywhere! bring your fishing rod ! After 6 hours of rafting which included a picnic and pitch stop, staff was waiting at the rendez vous spot , took care of our raft and unloaded all our belongings. Back to the starting point in a fancy bus/van, same courtesy from the driver. The cost was reasonable, I would recommend Sunshine Rafting to anyone looking for an unforgettable experience.</Review>

1603571944354</Date>
<Rate>2< /Rate>< review>
Finally went here because my husband loves Vallarta Supermarkets.  I was impressed with their selection of Latin American products.  If you need something, they probably have it here.  I bought a container of store made Mexican jello and guacamole.  Jello was just ok,  but the guacamole was really good.  Even at $7 a pound I am willing to keep going back for more.  The meat and deli selection is pretty good too they have several types of chorizo.
I didn't purchase anything from the hot food section because the line didn't look busy at dinner time which is not a good sign and the food looked a little on the dry side like it had been sitting out a minute.  The one area I was not impressed with was the pan dulce. Their pastries were just not good.  Their orejas (latin version of French oreilles) were on the salty side because they didn't put enough sugar on the pastry dough to caramelize it.  I bought an empanada de crema(or queso as the label it).  The custard filling needed more sugar I could taste the salt in it.  The dough/crust was also bland.  The biggest disappointment by far though was the pan "fino" that I purchased with a creme filling.  I cut it in half to share with my husband and the top crust was RAW.  I have been served dry, burnt, and under seasoned foods before but never have I been served a raw crust.

So there are some good things there and bad things here.  Great product and deli selection.  Guacamole is great, I will keep coming back for more.  But they need to get themselves a new panadero.</review>
